IF OBJECT_ID('[ADMINDB].[dbo].[tblBox_DirTree]', 'U') IS NOT NULL
	INSERT INTO [ADMINDB].[dbo].[tblBox_DirTree]([User_ID], [Body_ID], [IsTarget], [ToImport], [File_Path], [File_Name])
		SELECT d.[User_ID], d.[Body_ID], d.[IsTarget], d.[ToImport], d.[File_Path], d.[File_Name]
		FROM (SELECT 1, 8, 1, 1, f.parent_directory, f.file_or_directory_name
			FROM sys.dm_os_enumerate_filesystem(N'F:\Server\Ref\Import', N'*.*') f
			WHERE f.is_directory = 0
		) d([User_ID], [Body_ID], [IsTarget], [ToImport], [File_Path], [File_Name])
		LEFT JOIN [ADMINDB].[dbo].[tblBox_DirTree] [DT] ON d.[User_ID] = [DT].[User_ID]
			AND d.[Body_ID] = [DT].[Body_ID] AND d.[IsTarget] = [DT].[IsTarget] AND d.[ToImport] = [DT].[ToImport] AND d.[File_Path] = [DT].[File_Path] AND d.[File_Name] = [DT].[File_Name]
		WHERE [DT].ID IS NULL
		GROUP BY d.[User_ID], d.[Body_ID], d.[IsTarget], d.[ToImport], d.[File_Path], d.[File_Name]

EXEC sys.xp_delete_files 'F:\Server\Ref\Import\data\salesorder'

EXEC sys.xp_delete_files 'F:\Server\Ref\Import\Eco_Procept.Error.Txt'
IF OBJECT_ID('[ADMINDB].[dbo].[tblBox_Import]', 'U') IS NOT NULL
	AND OBJECT_ID('[ADMINDB].[dbo].[fnString_Split]', 'TF') IS NOT NULL
	INSERT INTO [ADMINDB].[dbo].[tblBox_Import]([DirTree_ID], [Column_ID], [Column_Name])
		SELECT x.[DirTree_ID], x.[Column_ID], x.[Column_Name]
		FROM (
			SELECT 1, s.[Nb], LEFT(s.[Split], 128)
			FROM (
				SELECT TOP 1 LEFT(BulkColumn, CHARINDEX(CHAR(10), BulkColumn)) FROM OPENROWSET(BULK N'F:\Server\Ref\Import\Abio_Metal.tsv', SINGLE_CLOB) x
			) x([Col])
			CROSS APPLY [ADMINDB].[dbo].[fnString_Split](REPLACE(REPLACE(x.[Col], CHAR(10), ''), CHAR(13), ''), '	') s
		) x([DirTree_ID], [Column_ID], [Column_Name])
		LEFT JOIN [ADMINDB].[dbo].[tblBox_Import] [BI] ON x.[DirTree_ID] = [BI].[DirTree_ID] AND x.[Column_ID] = [BI].[Column_ID] AND x.[Column_Name] = [BI].[Column_Name]
		WHERE [BI].ID IS NULL
		GROUP BY x.[DirTree_ID], x.[Column_ID], x.[Column_Name]

				SELECT TOP 1 LEFT(BulkColumn, CHARINDEX(CHAR(10), BulkColumn)) FROM OPENROWSET(BULK N'F:\Server\Ref\Import\data\arin_data_sets\arin_org.tsv', SINGLE_CLOB) x
			) x([Col])
			CROSS APPLY [ADMINDB].[dbo].[fnString_Split](REPLACE(REPLACE(x.[Col], CHAR(10), ''), CHAR(13), ''), '	') s
		) x([DirTree_ID], [Column_ID], [Column_Name])
		LEFT JOIN [ADMINDB].[dbo].[tblBox_Import] [BI] ON x.[DirTree_ID] = [BI].[DirTree_ID] AND x.[Column_ID] = [BI].[Column_ID] AND x.[Column_Name] = [BI].[Column_Name]
		WHERE [BI].ID IS NULL
		GROUP BY x.[DirTree_ID], x.[Column_ID], x.[Column_Name]
IF OBJECT_ID('[ADMINDB].[dbo].[tblBox_Import]', 'U') IS NOT NULL
	AND OBJECT_ID('[ADMINDB].[dbo].[fnString_Split]', 'TF') IS NOT NULL
	INSERT INTO [ADMINDB].[dbo].[tblBox_Import]([DirTree_ID], [Column_ID], [Column_Name])

			CROSS APPLY [ADMINDB].[dbo].[fnString_Split](REPLACE(REPLACE(x.[Col], CHAR(10), ''), CHAR(13), ''), ',') s
		) x([DirTree_ID], [Column_ID], [Column_Name])

		WHERE [BI].ID IS NULL
		GROUP BY x.[DirTree_ID], x.[Column_ID], x.[Column_Name]

IF OBJECT_ID('[ADMINDB].[dbo].[tblBox_System]', 'U') IS NOT NULL
	AND OBJECT_ID('[ADMINDB].[dbo].[tblBox_DirTree]', 'U') IS NOT NULL
	INSERT INTO [ADMINDB].[dbo].[tblBox_System]([User_ID]/*, [Object_ID]*/, [Level], [Name], [Description])
		SELECT [DT].[User_ID]/*, OBJECT_ID('[tempdb].[dbo].[##tbl' + [DT].[File_Path] + [DT].[File_Name] + ']', 'U')*/, 6, '##tbl' + [DT].[File_Path] + [DT].[File_Name], 'User''s object ' + [DT].[File_Path] + [DT].[File_Name]
		FROM [ADMINDB].[dbo].[tblBox_DirTree] [DT]
		INNER JOIN [ADMINDB].[dbo].[tblBox_File] [FL] ON RIGHT([DT].[File_Name], LEN('.' + [FL].[Extension])) = '.' + [FL].[Extension]
		LEFT JOIN [ADMINDB].[dbo].[tblBox_System] [BS] ON [DT].[User_ID] = [BS].[User_ID] AND '##tbl' + [DT].[File_Path] + [DT].[File_Name] = [BS].[Name]
		WHERE [DT].[User_ID] = 1 AND [DT].[ToImport] <> 0 AND [BS].ID IS NULL AND ISNULL([BS].[Level], 6) = 6
		GROUP BY [DT].[User_ID], [DT].[File_Path], [DT].[File_Name]
